187→\t\t\t\tadmissionmetrics.Metrics.ObserveWebhook(ctx, hook.Name, time.Since(t), rejected, versionedAttr.Attributes, \"admit\", 0)\n   188→\t\t\t}\n   189→\t\t} else {\n   190→\t\t\tadmissionmetrics.Metrics.ObserveWebhook(ctx, hook.Name, time.Since(t), rejected, versionedAttr.Attributes, \"admit\", 200)\n   191→\t\t}\n   192→\t\tif changed {\n   193→\t\t\t// Patch had 204→\t\tif callErr, ok := err.(*webhookutil.ErrCallingWebhook); ok {\n   205→\t\t\tif ignoreClientCallFailures {\n   206→\t\t\t\t// Ignore context cancelled from webhook metrics\n   207→\t\t\t\tif 218→\t\t\t\t\t// parent context is canceled or timed out, no point in continuing\n   219→\t\t\t\t\treturn apierrors.NewTimeoutError(\"request did not complete within requested timeout\", 0)\n callAttrMutatingHook updates attr\n   243→\n   244→func (a *mutatingDispatcher) callAttrMutatingHook(ctx context.Context, h *admissionregistrationv1.MutatingWebhook, invocation 404→\treturn &webhookAnnotator{\n   405→\t\tattr:                    attr,\n   406→\t\tfailedOpenAnnotationKey: fmt.Sprintf(\"%sround_%d_index_%d\", MutationAuditAnnotationFailedOpenKeyPrefix, round, *webhookAnnotator) addFailedOpenAnnotation() {\n   415→\tif w.attr == nil || w.attr.Attributes == nil {\n   416→\t\treturn\n   417→\t}\n   418→\tvalue := w.webhook\n   419→\tif err := w.failedOpenAnnotationKey, value, err)\n   421→\t}\n   422→}\n   423→\n   424→func (w *webhookAnnotator) addMutationAnnotation(mutated bool) {\n   425→\tif w.attr == nil || w.attr.Attributes == nil VerifyAdmissionResponse(uid types.UID, mutating bool, review runtime.Object) (*AdmissionResponse, error) {\n\tswitch r := review.(type) {\n\tcase *admissionv1.AdmissionReview:\n\t\tif r.Response == {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"webhook returned invalid response.patchType of %q\", patchType)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t// Ensure a validating webhook doesn't return patch or patchType\n\t\t\tif len(r.Response.Patch) > 0 {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"validating webhook may not return response.patch\")\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif r.Response.PatchType != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn   r.Response.Allowed,\n\t\t\tPatch:            patch,\n\t\t\tPatchType:        patchType,\n\t\t\tResult:           r.Response.Result,\n\t\t\tWarnings:         r.Response.Warnings,\n\t\t}, admissionv1.PatchTypeJSONPatch\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\treturn &AdmissionResponse{\n\t\t\tAuditAnnotations: r.Response.AuditAnnotations,\n\t\t\tAllowed:          r.Response.Allowed,\n\t\t\tPatch:            patch,\n\t\t\tPatchType:        patchType,\n\t\t\tResult:           r.Response.Result,\n\t\t\tWarnings:         r.Response.Warnings,\n\t\t}, nil\n\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unexpected response type %T\", review)\n\t}\n}\n\n// CreateAdmissionObjects returns the unique request uid, the AdmissionReview object to send the webhook and to decode the response in kubernetes/kubernetes at staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/. The chain consists of two separate admission controllers: MutatingAdmissionWebhook and ValidatingAdmissionWebhook, which are registered in mutating/plugin.go and validating/plugin.go respectively.\\n\\n## Chain Architecture\\n\\n### 1. Webhook Admission Controllers\\nBoth mutating and validating webhook plugins (mutating/plugin.go and validating/plugin.go) implement the admission.Interface. The mutating plugin's Admit() method and the validating plugin's Validate() method both delegate to the generic Webhook.Dispatch() method in generic/webhook.go.\\n\\n### 2. Generic Webhook Framework\\nThe core webhook logic is in generic/webhook.go. The Webhook struct orchestrates:\\n- **Dispatch()**: Entry point that calls the dispatcher with hooks from the webhook source\\n- **ShouldCallHook()**: Evaluates whether a specific webhook should be called based on:\\n  - Namespace selector matching (predicates/namespace/matcher.go)\\n  - Object selector matching (predicates/object/matcher.go)\\n  - Rule matching against the request (predicates/rules/rules.go)\\n  - CEL condition matching (matchconditions/matcher.go)\\n\\n### 3. Webhook Configuration Management\\nWebhooks are dynamically loaded from the Kubernetes API:\\n- mutating_webhook_manager.go: Manages MutatingWebhookConfigurations via informers\\n- validating_webhook_manager.go: Manages ValidatingWebhookConfigurations via informers\\n\\nBoth managers implement the generic.Source interface and wrap webhooks with WebhookAccessor (accessors.go) to provide a uniform interface.\\n\\n### 4. Dispatcher Layer - Execution Strategies\\n\\n**Mutating Webhooks (mutating/dispatcher.go)**:\\n- Executes webhooks sequentially in order\\n- For each webhook, calls callAttrMutatingHook() which:\\n  - Creates AdmissionReview request objects (request/admissionreview.go)\\n  - Makes HTTP POST call to the webhook endpoint via REST client\\n  - Verifies the response (VerifyAdmissionResponse)\\n  - Applies JSON patches from the response to the object\\n  - Handles reinvocation if patches modify the object (mutating/reinvocationcontext.go)\\n  - Aggregates audit annotations and warnings\\n\\n**Validating Webhooks (validating/dispatcher.go)**:\\n- Executes webhooks in parallel using goroutines\\n- For each webhook, calls callHook() which:\\n  - Creates AdmissionReview request objects\\n  - Makes HTTP POST call to the webhook endpoint\\n  - Verifies the response\\n  - Rejects the request if any webhook denies it\\n  - Handles failure policies (fail closed/open)\\n\\n### 5. Request/Response Handling\\nThe request/admissionreview.go file contains:\\n- **CreateAdmissionObjects()**: Converts API server attributes to AdmissionReview requests (v1 and v1beta1)\\n- **VerifyAdmissionResponse()**: Validates webhook responses and extracts patches, decisions, and audit annotations\\n- **CreateV1AdmissionReview()** and **CreateV1beta1AdmissionReview()**: Build request objects with versioned object representations\\n\\n### 6. Error Handling and Aggregation\\nErrors and responses are aggregated:\\n- errors/statuserror.go: Converts webhook denial responses to appropriate HTTP status errors\\n- Both dispatchers track rejection metrics and handle failure policies\\n- Mutating dispatcher annotates audit log with patch information\\n- Validating dispatcher collects and returns the first error in parallel execution\\n\\n### 7. Supporting Infrastructure\\n- **Webhook Accessors** (accessors.go): Provide uniform interface to MutatingWebhook and ValidatingWebhook objects, handling lazy initialization and CEL matcher compilation\\n- **Initializer** (initializer/initializer.go): Sets up informers and other dependencies\\n- **Config** (config/kubeconfig.go): Loads kubeconfig for webhook client authentication\\n\\n## Execution Flow Summary\\n\\n1. API server calls Admit() or Validate() on the respective plugin\\n2. Plugin delegates to generic Webhook.Dispatch()\\n3. Dispatch retrieves webhooks from configuration manager (mutating/validating_webhook_manager.go)\\n4. For each webhook, ShouldCallHook() evaluates predicates and conditions\\n5. Matching webhooks are dispatched to the appropriate dispatcher:\\n   - Mutating: Sequential execution with patch aggregation and reinvocation support\\n   - Validating: Parallel execution with fast-fail semantics\\n6. Request/Response handling creates AdmissionReview objects and verifies responses\\n7. in kubernetes/kubernetes at staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/. The chain consists of two separate admission controllers: MutatingAdmissionWebhook and ValidatingAdmissionWebhook, which are registered in mutating/plugin.go and validating/plugin.go respectively.\\n\\n## Chain Architecture\\n\\n### 1. Webhook Admission Controllers\\nBoth mutating and validating webhook plugins (mutating/plugin.go and validating/plugin.go) implement the admission.Interface. The mutating plugin's Admit() method and the validating plugin's Validate() method both delegate to the generic Webhook.Dispatch() method in generic/webhook.go.\\n\\n### 2. Generic Webhook Framework\\nThe core webhook logic is in generic/webhook.go. The Webhook struct orchestrates:\\n- **Dispatch()**: Entry point that calls the dispatcher with hooks from the webhook source\\n- **ShouldCallHook()**: Evaluates whether a specific webhook should be called based on:\\n  - Namespace selector matching (predicates/namespace/matcher.go)\\n  - Object selector matching (predicates/object/matcher.go)\\n  - Rule matching against the request (predicates/rules/rules.go)\\n  - CEL condition matching (matchconditions/matcher.go)\\n\\n### 3. Webhook Configuration Management\\nWebhooks are dynamically loaded from the Kubernetes API:\\n- mutating_webhook_manager.go: Manages MutatingWebhookConfigurations via informers\\n- validating_webhook_manager.go: Manages ValidatingWebhookConfigurations via informers\\n\\nBoth managers implement the generic.Source interface and wrap webhooks with WebhookAccessor (accessors.go) to provide a uniform interface.\\n\\n### 4. Dispatcher Layer - Execution Strategies\\n\\n**Mutating Webhooks (mutating/dispatcher.go)**:\\n- Executes webhooks sequentially in order\\n- For each webhook, calls callAttrMutatingHook() which:\\n  - Creates AdmissionReview request objects (request/admissionreview.go)\\n  - Makes HTTP POST call to the webhook endpoint via REST client\\n  - Verifies the response (VerifyAdmissionResponse)\\n  - Applies JSON patches from the response to the object\\n  - Handles reinvocation if patches modify the object (mutating/reinvocationcontext.go)\\n  - Aggregates audit annotations and warnings\\n\\n**Validating Webhooks (validating/dispatcher.go)**:\\n- Executes webhooks in parallel using goroutines\\n- For each webhook, calls callHook() which:\\n  - Creates AdmissionReview request objects\\n  - Makes HTTP POST call to the webhook endpoint\\n  - Verifies the response\\n  - Rejects the request if any webhook denies it\\n  - Handles failure policies (fail closed/open)\\n\\n### 5. Request/Response Handling\\nThe request/admissionreview.go file contains:\\n- **CreateAdmissionObjects()**: Converts API server attributes to AdmissionReview requests (v1 and v1beta1)\\n- **VerifyAdmissionResponse()**: Validates webhook responses and extracts patches, decisions, and audit annotations\\n- **CreateV1AdmissionReview()** and **CreateV1beta1AdmissionReview()**: Build request objects with versioned object representations\\n\\n### 6. Error Handling and Aggregation\\nErrors and responses are aggregated:\\n- errors/statuserror.go: Converts webhook denial responses to appropriate HTTP status errors\\n- Both dispatchers track rejection metrics and handle failure policies\\n- Mutating dispatcher annotates audit log with patch information\\n- Validating dispatcher collects and returns the first error in parallel execution\\n\\n### 7. Supporting Infrastructure\\n- **Webhook Accessors** (accessors.go): Provide uniform interface to MutatingWebhook and ValidatingWebhook objects, handling lazy initialization and CEL matcher compilation\\n- **Initializer** (initializer/initializer.go): Sets up informers and other dependencies\\n- **Config** (config/kubeconfig.go): Loads kubeconfig for webhook client authentication\\n\\n## Execution Flow Summary\\n\\n1. API server calls Admit() or Validate() on the respective plugin\\n2. Plugin delegates to generic Webhook.Dispatch()\\n3. Dispatch retrieves webhooks from configuration manager (mutating/validating_webhook_manager.go)\\n4. For each webhook, ShouldCallHook() evaluates predicates and conditions\\n5. Matching webhooks are dispatched to the appropriate dispatcher:\\n   - Mutating: Sequential execution with patch aggregation and reinvocation support\\n   - Validating: Parallel execution with fast-fail semantics\\n6. Request/Response handling creates AdmissionReview objects and verifies responses\\n7. Errors are converted and propagated, or requests are allowed/denied based on webhook decisions\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
